<p>By <a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/cloud_and_mobile/philippe-leefsma.html">Philippe Leefsma</a></p>  <p>In my <a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/cloud_and_mobile/2014/08/autodesk-view-data-api-javascript-wrapper.html">previous post</a> I was exposing a JavaScript wrapper for the View &amp; Data which makes it easy to upload and translate your files from a client html page.</p>  <p>I’ve been playing with the <a href="http://developer.api.autodesk.com/documentation/v1/viewers/index.html">Viewer API</a> for couple of months now and I found it useful to use a little wrapper around the client API, so common tasks such as loading/closing a document, saving/restoring a view, getting a property value are more straightforward.</p>  <p>Here is the most basic example on how to use the wrapper:</p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><font face="Consolas"><span lang="FR" style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white; mso-ansi-language: fr"><font color="#000000"><font style="font-size: 9.5pt">$(document).ready(</font></font></span><font style="font-size: 9.5pt"><span lang="FR" style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white; mso-ansi-language: fr"><font color="#0000ff">function</font></span></font><span lang="FR" style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white; mso-ansi-language: fr"><font style="font-size: 9.5pt" color="#000000"> () {</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span lang="FR" style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white; mso-ansi-language: fr"><font face="Consolas"><font style="font-size: 9.5pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><font face="Consolas"><span lang="FR" style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white; mso-ansi-language: fr"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000"><font style="font-size: 9.5pt">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span><span lang="FR" style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white; mso-ansi-language: fr"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white"><font face="Consolas"><font style="font-size: 9.5pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white"><font style="font-size: 9.5pt" color="#008000">// loads document</font></span></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><span style="font-family: ; background-image: none; background-repeat: repeat; background-attachment: scroll; background-position: 0% 0%; color: ; mso-highlight: white"><font color="#000000" face="Consolas"></font></span></p>  <p>A concrete example can be found in my <a href="https://github.com/Developer-Autodesk/workflow-node.js-view.and.data.api">Node.js Sample</a>.</p>  <p>Below is the current code of that wrapper, but you will find the up-to-date version on github, so I recommend you grab this one instead:</p>  <p><a href="https://github.com/Developer-Autodesk/library-javascript-view.and.data.api/blob/master/js/Autodesk.ADN.Toolkit.Viewer.js">Autodesk.ADN.Toolkit.Viewer.js on Github</a></p>  <p><font color="#ffffff">-</font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt;         #viewer2 {

            margin:25px;
            width: 440px;
            position: relative;
            overflow: hidden;

            border: 1px solid #cccccc;

    </style>      <script type="text/javascript" src="http://code.jquery.com/jquery-2.1.1.js"></script>          <!--///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
    // Viewer
    //
    ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////-->     <link type="text/css" rel="stylesheet" href="https://viewing.api.autodesk.com/viewingservice/v1/viewers/style.css" />     <script type="text/javascript" src="https://developer.api.autodesk.com/viewingservice/v1/viewers/viewer3D.min.js"></script>     <script type="text/javascript" src="https://rawgit.com/Developer-Autodesk/library-javascript-view.and.data.api/master/js/Autodesk.ADN.Toolkit.ViewData.js"></script>     <script type="text/javascript" src="https://rawgit.com/Developer-Autodesk/library-javascript-view.and.data.api/master/js/Autodesk.ADN.Toolkit.Viewer.js"></script>        <script type='text/javascript'>

        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // 
        //
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        var files2 = [];

        var viewDataClient2;

        var adnViewerMng2;

        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // 
        //
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        function testApi() {

            //sanity checks ...
            var token = $('#token2').val();

            if (token === '') {
                console.log('Access Token cannot be empty');
                console.log('Exiting ...');
                return;
            }

            var bucket = $('#bucket2').val();

            if (bucket === '') {
                console.log('Bucket name cannot be empty');
                console.log('Exiting ...');
                return;
            }

            if (files2.length === 0) {
                console.log('No file to upload');
                console.log('Exiting ...');
                return;
            }

            //get into business
            viewDataClient2 = new Autodesk.ADN.Toolkit.ViewData.AdnViewDataClient(
              'https://developer.api.autodesk.com',
              token);

            viewDataClient2.getBucketDetailsAsync(

                bucket,

                //onSuccess
                function (bucketResponse) {

                    console.log('Bucket details successful:');
                    console.log(bucketResponse);

                    uploadFiles(bucket, files2);
                },

                //onError
                function (error) {

                    console.log("Bucket doesn't exist");
                    console.log("Attempting to create...");

                    createBucket(bucket);
                });
        }

        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // 
        //
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        function createBucket(bucket) {

            var bucketCreationData = {
                bucketKey: bucket,
                servicesAllowed: {},
                policy: 'transient'
            }

            viewDataClient2.createBucketAsync(

                bucketCreationData,

                //onSuccess
                function (response) {

                    console.log('Bucket creation successful:');
                    console.log(response);

                    uploadFiles(response.key, files2);
                },

                //onError
                function (error) {

                    console.log('Bucket creation failed:');
                    console.log(error);
                    console.log('Exiting ...');
                    return;
                });
        }

        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // 
        //
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        function uploadFiles(bucket, files) {

            for (var i = 0; i < files.length; ++i) {

                var file = files[i];

                console.log('Uploading file: ' + file.name + ' ...');

                viewDataClient2.uploadFileAsync(

                    file,
                    bucket,
                    file.name,

                    //onSuccess
                    function (response) {

                        console.log('File upload successful:');
                        console.log(response);

                        var fileId = response.objects[0].id;

                        var registerResponse =
                            viewDataClient2.register(fileId);

                        if (registerResponse.Result === "Success" ||
		            registerResponse.Result === "Created") {

                            console.log("Registration result: " +
                                registerResponse.Result);

                            console.log('Starting translation: ' +
                                fileId);

                            checkTranslationStatus(
                                fileId,
                                1000 * 60 * 5, //5 mins timeout

                                //onSuccess
                                function (viewable) {

                                    console.log("Translation successful: " +
                                        response.file.name);

                                    console.log("Viewable: ");
                                    console.log(viewable);

                                    adnViewerMng2 = new Autodesk.ADN.Toolkit.Viewer.AdnViewerManager(
                                        $('#token2').val(),
                                        document.getElementById('viewer2'));

                                    adnViewerMng2.loadDocument(viewable.urn);
                                });
                        }
                    },

                    //onError
                    function (error) {

                        console.log('File upload failed:');
                        console.log(error);
                    });
            }
        }

        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // 
        //
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        function checkTranslationStatus(fileId, timeout, onSuccess) {

            var startTime = new Date().getTime();

            var timer = setInterval(function () {

                var dt = (new Date().getTime() - startTime) / timeout;

                if (dt >= 1.0) {

                    clearInterval(timer);
                }
                else {

                    viewDataClient2.getViewableAsync(
                        fileId,
                        function (response) {

                            console.log(
                                'Translation Progess ' +
                                fileId + ': '
                                + response.progress);

                            if (response.progress === 'complete') {

                                clearInterval(timer);
                                onSuccess(response);
                            }
                        },
                        function (error) {

                        });
                }
            }, 2000);
        };

        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // 
        //
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        function onFileSelect(event) {

            files2 = event.target.files;

            var output = [];

            for (var i = 0; i < files2.length; ++i) {

                var file = files2[i]

                output.push(
                    '<li><strong>',
                    escape(file.name),
                    '</strong> (',
                    file.type || 'n/a',
                    ') <br>',
                    file.size,
                    ' bytes, last modified: ',
                    file.lastModifiedDate ? file.lastModifiedDate.toLocaleDateString() : 'n/a',
                    '</li><br>');
            }

            document.getElementById('fileList2').innerHTML = '<ul>' + output.join('') + '</ul>';
        }
      
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        // 
        //
        ///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
        $().ready(function () {

            document.getElementById('fileInput2').addEventListener(
                'change',
                onFileSelect,
                false);
        });

    </script>      <div class="roundedArea">          <strong>ADN View & Data API Tester</strong>          <br><br>         Input the name of a bucket and select files to upload. If the bucket doesn't exist it will be created,          then the files will be upload and translated, ready for viewing using the output URN.          <br><br>         Token generation cannot be achieved from a browser, so you need API keys to generate the token some other way:          using curl, an executable, ADN samples, ...              <br><br>         Access Token:          <br>         <input type="text" id="token2">          <br><br>         Bucket name:          <br>         <input type="text" id="bucket2">      </div>      <div class="roundedArea">         Select file to upload...         <br><br>                  <input type="file" id="fileInput2" name="files[]"/>                  <output id="fileList2"></output>     </div>      <div class="roundedArea">             <button type="button" onclick="testApi()">Let's view it!</button>     </div>      <div id="viewer2" style="height:400px;">      </div>
